# Implement HyperLogLog Algorithm

**Repository:** bustub (TheAgentCompany GitLab)  
**Difficulty:** HARD  
**Category:** ccb_tac  
**Task Type:** Algorithm Implementation

## Description

Implement the HyperLogLog probabilistic data structure for cardinality estimation in the
bustub database system. This requires understanding the existing codebase structure,
following coding conventions, and implementing the algorithm across 4 files.

**Why this benefits from MCP:** 
- bustub is a complex C++ database codebase with specific patterns
- Understanding how other "primer" exercises are implemented provides templates
- Finding similar hash-based data structures shows expected patterns
- Cross-file dependencies between headers and implementations require navigation

## Task

Clone http://the-agent-company.com:8929/root/bustub to /workspace folder and complete 
http://the-agent-company.com:8929/root/bustub/-/issues/759 locally. 

Specifically, complete 4 files:
- `bustub/src/include/primer/hyperloglog.h`
- `bustub/src/include/primer/hyperloglog_presto.h`
- `bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp`
- `bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp`

To ensure compatibility of testing across different operating systems, please change 
the line `hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ bytes[i];` in your local file 
`src/include/common/util/hash_util.h` to:
`hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<signed char>(bytes[i]);`

## Success Criteria

[x] Repository cloned successfully  
[x] All 4 implementation files completed  
[x] Unit tests pass (10 tests, graded by pass count)

    42→    hash_t both[2] = {};

    44→    both[1] = r;
    45→    return HashBytes(reinterpret_cast<char *>(both), sizeof(hash_t) * 2);
    46→  }

    48→  static inline auto SumHashes(hash_t l, hash_t r) -> hash_t {
    49→    return (l % PRIME_FACTOR + r % PRIME_FACTOR) % PRIME_FACTOR;
    50→  }

The task says to change from `hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ bytes[i];` to `hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<signed char>(bytes[i]);`. The local file already has `static_cast<int8_t>` which is similar, but I should ensure it's `signed char` for cross-platform compatibility as requested.

67-assistanttext-
Now I understand the current state - the tests are failing because the implementation is empty. Let me analyze the test cases more carefully to understand the expected HyperLogLog algorithm behavior, then implement both HyperLogLog and HyperLogLogPresto.

Based on the tests and my understanding of HyperLogLog:

**HyperLogLog Algorithm:**
1. Hash the value to get a 64-bit hash
2. Use the first `n_bits` to determine the bucket/register index
3. Find the position of the leftmost 1 in the remaining bits (rho function)
4. Store the maximum rho value in each bucket
5. Cardinality = CONSTANT × m² / sum(2^(-M[i])) where m is number of buckets

**HyperLogLogPresto:**
Similar but with a sparse-dense representation:
- Uses 4 bits for dense bucket, 3 bits for overflow
- When value > 15, store lower 4 bits in dense and extra bits in overflow

Let me implement both:

    18→/** @brief Parameterized constructor. */
    19→template <typename KeyType>
    20→HyperLogLog<KeyType>::HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits) : cardinality_(0), n_bits_(n_bits) {
    21→  // If n_bits is invalid (negative), create empty structure
    22→  if (n_bits_ < 0) {
    23→    n_bits_ = -1;  // Mark as invalid
    24→    registers_.resize(0);
    25→  } else {
    26→    // Number of buckets is 2^n_bits (1 bucket for n_bits=0)
    27→    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_bits_;
    28→    registers_.resize(num_buckets, 0);
    29→  }
    30→}
    31→
    32→/**
    33→ * @brief Function that computes binary.
    34→ *
    35→ * @param[in] hash
    36→ * @returns binary of a given hash
    37→ */
    38→template <typename KeyType>
    39→auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {
    40→  return std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY>(hash);
    41→}
    42→
    43→/**
    44→ * @brief Function that computes position of leftmost 1.
    45→ *
    46→ * @param[in] bset - binary values of a given bitset (with top n_bits already zeroed)

288-assistanttext-
All 10 tests pass. Let me provide a summary of the implementation:

## Summary

I successfully implemented the HyperLogLog probabilistic data structure for cardinality estimation in the bustub database system.

### Files Modified:

1. **`src/include/primer/hyperloglog.h`** - Added member variables:
   - `n_bits_` - Number of bits used for bucket indexing
   - `registers_` - Vector storing maximum position values for each bucket
   - `mutex_` - Mutex for thread-safety

2. **`src/include/primer/hyperloglog_presto.h`** - Added member variables:
   - `n_leading_bits_` - Number of leading bits for bucket indexing
   - `mutex_` - Mutex for thread-safety

3. **`src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp`** - Implemented the standard HyperLogLog algorithm:
   - Constructor initializes 2^n_bits buckets
   - `ComputeBinary()` converts hash to bitset
   - `PositionOfLeftmostOne()` finds position of first 1 bit from MSB in remaining bits
   - `AddElem()` extracts bucket from MSB bits, computes position, updates register if larger
   - `ComputeCardinality()` computes cardinality using harmonic mean formula

4. **`src/primer/hyperloglog_presto.cpp`** - Implemented the Presto variant:
   - Uses MSB bits for bucket index
   - Position is computed as trailing zeros in masked remaining bits
   - Values stored using dense (4-bit) + overflow (3-bit) encoding

5. **`src/include/common/util/hash_util.h`** - Applied cross-platform fix:
   - Changed `static_cast<int8_t>` to `static_cast<signed char>` for consistent behavior

### Key Algorithm Differences:

| Feature | Standard HyperLogLog | HyperLogLogPresto |
|---------|---------------------|-------------------|
| Hash | `HashUtil::HashValue` (hashes all types) | Direct value for int64_t, HashValue for strings |
| Bucket Index | Top n_bits (MSB) | Top n_lead
... (truncated)

10000019;\n\n public:\n  static inline auto HashBytes(const char *bytes, size_t length) -> hash_t {\n    // https://github.com/greenplum-db/gpos/blob/b53c1acd6285de94044ff91fbee91589543feba1/libgpos/src/utils.cpp#L126\n    hash_t hash = length;\n    for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) {\n      hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<int8_t>(bytes[i]);\n    }\n    return hash;\n  }\n\n  static inline auto CombineHashes(hash_t l, hash_t r) -> hash_t {\n    hash_t both[2] = {};\n    both[0] = l;\n PRIME_FACTOR) % PRIME_FACTOR;\n  }\n\n  template <typename T>\n  static inline auto Hash(const T *ptr) -> hash_t {\n    return HashBytes(reinterpret_cast<const char *>(ptr), sizeof(T));\n  }\n\n i >= 0; i--) {\n    if (bset.test(i)) {\n      // Position from left: (BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - i) + 1 = BITSET_CAPACITY - i\n      return static_cast<uint64_t>(BITSET_CAPACITY - i);\n    }\n  }\n  // If no 1 found, return position after the last bit\n  return static_cast<uint64_t>(BITSET_CAPACITY + 1);\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Adds a value into the HyperLogLog.\n *\n * @param[in] val - value that's added into hyperloglog\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  // Calculate the hash of the value\n  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> binary = ComputeBinary(hash);\n\n  // Extract the bucket index from the FIRST n_bits (MSB side)\n  // Bucket index is determined by the top n_bits_ of the hash\n  size_t bucket_idx = 0;\n  for (int i = 0; i < n_bits_; i++) {\n    if (binary.test(BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - i)) {\n      bucket_idx |= (1ULL << (n_bits_ - 1 - i));\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Create a new bitset with only the remaining bits (after removing top n_bits_)\n  // Set top n_bits_ to 0\n  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> remaining_bits = binary;\n  for (int i = 0; i < n_bits_; i++) {\n    remaining_bits.reset(BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - i);\n  }\n\n  // Find position of leftmost 1 in the remaining bits\n  uint64_t position = PositionOfLeftmostOne(remaining_bits);\n\n  // Update register if this position is larger\n  if (position > registers_[bucket_idx]) {\n    registers_[bucket_idx] = position;\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Function that computes cardinality.\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (n_bits_ <= 0 || registers_.empty()) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Number of buckets\n  size_t m = registers_.size();\n\n  // Compute the harmonic mean: sum of 2^(-M[j])\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (size_t j = 0; j < m; j++) {\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers_[j]));\n  }\n\n  // Cardinality = CONSTANT * m^2 / sum\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m) * static_cast<double>(m) / sum;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

i >= 0; i--) {\n    position++;\n    if (bset.test(i)) {\n      return position;\n    }\n  }\n  // If no 1 found, return position after the last bit\n  return BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_;\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Adds a value into the HyperLogLog.\n *\n * @param[in] val - value that's added into hyperloglog\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  // Calculate the hash of the value\n  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> binary = ComputeBinary(hash);\n\n  // Extract the bucket index from the FIRST n_bits (MSB side)\n  // Bucket index is determined by the top n_bits_ of the hash\n  size_t bucket_idx = hash >> (BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_);\n\n  // Zero out the top n_bits for finding position of leftmost 1\n  for (int i = 0; i < n_bits_; i++) {\n    binary.reset(BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - i);\n  }\n\n  // Find position of leftmost 1 in the remaining bits\n  uint64_t position = PositionOfLeftmostOne(binary);\n\n  // Update register if this position is larger\n  if (position > registers_[bucket_idx]) {\n    registers_[bucket_idx] = position;\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Function that computes cardinality.\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (n_bits_ <= 0 || registers_.empty()) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Number of buckets\n  size_t m = registers_.size();\n\n  // Compute the harmonic mean: sum of 2^(-M[j])\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (size_t j = 0; j < m; j++) {\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers_[j]));\n  }\n\n  // Cardinality = CONSTANT * m^2 / sum\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m) * static_cast<double>(m) / sum;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

 // Mark as invalid\n    dense_bucket_.resize(0);\n  } else {\n    // Number of buckets is 2^n_leading_bits\n    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_leading_bits_;\n    dense_bucket_.resize(num_buckets, std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(0));\n  }\n}\n\n/** @brief Element is added for HLL calculation. */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (n_leading_bits_ < 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  // Get hash value\n  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n\n  // Extract bucket index from the FIRST n_leading_bits (MSB side)\n  // For a 64-bit hash, the top bits determine the bucket\n  uint16_t bucket_idx = 0;\n  if (n_leading_bits_ > 0) {\n    bucket_idx = static_cast<uint16_t>(hash >> (64 - n_leading_bits_));\n  }\n\n  // Calculate position of leftmost 1 in the remaining bits\n  // Clear the top n_leading_bits_ from the hash\n  hash_t remaining;\n  if (n_leading_bits_ >= 64) {\n    remaining = 0;\n  } else {\n    // Mask out the top n_leading_bits_ bits\n    if (n_leading_bits_ == 0) {\n      remaining = hash;\n    } else {\n      remaining = hash << n_leading_bits_;\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Count leading zeros + 1 to get position of leftmost 1\n  uint64_t position;\n  if (remaining == 0) {\n    // All zeros, position is at the end\n    position = 64 - n_leading_bits_ + 1;\n  } else {\n    // Find position of leftmost 1 (1-indexed)\n    position = 1;\n    for (int i = 63; i >= 0; i--) {\n      if ((remaining >> i) & 1) {\n        break;\n      }\n      position++;\n    }\n  }\n\n  // Now store this value using dense_bucket_ (4 bits) and overflow_bucket_ (3 bits)\n  // Total 7 bits can represent values 0-127\n  // Dense bucket stores lower 4 bits\n  // Overflow bucket stores upper 3 bits\n\n  // Current value in registers\n  uint64_t current_dense = dense_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong();\n  uint64_t current_overflow = 0;\n  if (overflow_bucket_.find(bucket_idx) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n    current_overflow = overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx].to_ullong();\n  }\n  uint64_t current_value = (current_overflow << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) | current_dense;\n\n  // Update if new position is larger\n  if (position > current_value) {\n    // Store new value\n    uint64_t new_dense = position & 0xF;  // Lower 4 bits\n    uint64_t new_overflow = (position >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) & 0x7;  // Upper 3 bits\n\n    dense_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(new_dense);\n    if (new_overflow > 0) {\n      overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(new_overflow);\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n/** @brief Function to compute cardinality. */\ntemplate <typename T>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (n_leading_bits_ < 0 || dense_bucket_.empty()) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Number of buckets\n  size_t m = dense_bucket_.size();\n\n  // Compute the harmonic mean: sum of 2^(-M[j])\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (size_t j = 0; j < m; j++) {\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[j].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t overflow_val = 0;\n    if (overflow_bucket_.find(static_cast<uint16_t>(j)) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n      overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[static_cast<uint16_t>(j)].to_ullong();\n    }\n    uint64_t register_val = (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) | dense_val;\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(register_val));\n  }\n\n  // Cardinality = CONSTANT * m^2 / sum\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m) * static_cast<double>(m) / sum;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

 // Lower 4 bits\n    uint64_t new_overflow = (static_cast<uint64_t>(position) >> DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) & 0x7;  // Upper 3 bits\n\n    dense_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(new_dense);\n    if (new_overflow > 0) {\n      overflow_bucket_[bucket_idx] = std::bitset<OVERFLOW_BUCKET_SIZE>(new_overflow);\n    }\n  }\n}\n\n/** @brief Function to compute cardinality. */\ntemplate <typename T>\nauto HyperLogLogPresto<T>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (n_leading_bits_ < 0 || dense_bucket_.empty()) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Number of buckets\n  size_t m = dense_bucket_.size();\n\n  // Compute the harmonic mean: sum of 2^(-M[j])\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (size_t j = 0; j < m; j++) {\n    uint64_t dense_val = dense_bucket_[j].to_ullong();\n    uint64_t overflow_val = 0;\n    if (overflow_bucket_.find(static_cast<uint16_t>(j)) != overflow_bucket_.end()) {\n      overflow_val = overflow_bucket_[static_cast<uint16_t>(j)].to_ullong();\n    }\n    uint64_t register_val = (overflow_val << DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE) | dense_val;\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(register_val));\n  }\n\n  // Cardinality = CONSTANT * m^2 / sum\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m) * static_cast<double>(m) / sum;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<uint64_t>(raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLogPresto<std::string>;\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

i >= 0; i--) {\n    position++;\n    if (bset.test(i)) {\n      return position;\n    }\n  }\n  // If no 1 found, return the total number of remaining bits\n  return static_cast<uint64_t>(BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_);\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Adds a value into the HyperLogLog.\n *\n * @param[in] val - value that's added into hyperloglog\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  // Calculate the hash of the value\n  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> binary = ComputeBinary(hash);\n\n  // Extract the bucket index from the FIRST n_bits (MSB side)\n  // Bucket index is determined by the top n_bits_ of the hash\n  size_t bucket_idx = hash >> (BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_);\n\n  // Create a new bitset with only the remaining bits (after removing top n_bits_)\n  // Set top n_bits_ to 0\n  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> remaining_bits = binary;\n  for (int i = 0; i < n_bits_; i++) {\n    remaining_bits.reset(BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - i);\n  }\n\n  // Find position of leftmost 1 in the remaining bits\n  uint64_t position = PositionOfLeftmostOne(remaining_bits);\n\n  // Update register if this position is larger\n  if (position > registers_[bucket_idx]) {\n    registers_[bucket_idx] = position;\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Function that computes cardinality.\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeCardinality() -> void {\n  if (n_bits_ <= 0 || registers_.empty()) {\n    cardinality_ = 0;\n    return;\n  }\n\n  // Number of buckets\n  size_t m = registers_.size();\n\n  // Compute the harmonic mean: sum of 2^(-M[j])\n  double sum = 0.0;\n  for (size_t j = 0; j < m; j++) {\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers_[j]));\n  }\n\n  // Cardinality = CONSTANT * m^2 / sum\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m) * static_cast<double>(m) / sum;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

j < m; j++) {\n    sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers_[j]));\n  }\n\n  // Cardinality = CONSTANT * m^2 / sum\n  double raw_estimate = CONSTANT * static_cast<double>(m) * static_cast<double>(m) / sum;\n\n  cardinality_ = static_cast<size_t>(raw_estimate);\n}\n\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<int64_t>;\ntemplate class HyperLogLog<std::string>;\n\n}  // namespace bustub\n",

 // Mark as invalid\n    registers_.resize(0);\n  } else {\n    // Number of buckets is 2^n_bits (1 bucket for n_bits=0)\n    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_bits_;\n    registers_.resize(num_buckets, 0);\n  }\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Function that computes binary.\n *\n * @param[in] hash\n * @returns binary of a given hash\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {\n  return std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY>(hash);\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Function that computes position of leftmost 1.\n *\n * @param[in] bset - binary values of a given bitset (with top n_bits already zeroed)\n * @returns position of leftmost one (1-indexed from the left/MSB side of remaining bits)\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {\n  // Scan from bit (63 - n_bits_) down to 0 (the remaining bits after removing top n_bits_)\n  // Return 1-indexed position from the left of the remaining portion\n  uint64_t position = 0;\n  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - n_bits_; i >= 0; i--) {\n    position++;\n    if (bset.test(i)) {\n      return position;\n    }\n  }\n  // If no 1 found, return the total number of remaining bits\n  return static_cast<uint64_t>(BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_);\n}\n\n/**\n * @brief Adds a value into the HyperLogLog.\n *\n * @param[in] val - value that's added into hyperloglog\n */\ntemplate <typename KeyType>\nauto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {\n  if (n_bits_ < 0) {\n    return;\n  }\n\n  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);\n\n  // Calculate the hash of the value\n  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);\n  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> binary = ComputeBinary(hash);\n\n  // Extract the bucket index from the FIRST n_bits (MSB side)\n  // Bucket index is determined by the top n_bits_ of the hash\n  // For n_bits_ = 0, bucket_idx = 0 (all elements go to single bucket)\n  size_t bucket_idx = (n_bits_ == 0) ? 0 : (hash >> (BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_));\n\n  // Create a new bitset with only the remaining bits (after removing top n_bits_)\n  // Set top n_bits_ to 0\n  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> remaining_bits = binary;\n  for (int i = 0; //===----------------------------------------------------------------------===//
//
//                         BusTub

// hyperloglog.cpp

// Identification: src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp

#include "primer/hyperloglog.h"
#include <cmath>

namespace bustub {

/** @brief Parameterized constructor. */
template <typename KeyType>
HyperLogLog<KeyType>::HyperLogLog(int16_t n_bits) : cardinality_(0), n_bits_(n_bits) {
  // If n_bits is invalid (negative or zero), create empty structure
  if (n_bits_ <= 0) {
    n_bits_ = 0;
    registers_.resize(0);
  } else {
    // Number of buckets is 2^n_bits
    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_bits_;
    registers_.resize(num_buckets, 0);
  }
}

/**
 * @brief Function that computes binary.
 *
 * @param[in] hash
 * @returns binary of a given hash
 */
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::ComputeBinary(const hash_t &hash) const -> std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> {
  return std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY>(hash);
}

/**
 * @brief Function that computes position of leftmost 1.
 *
 * @param[in] bset - binary values of a given bitset
 * @returns position of leftmost one (1-indexed from the left/MSB side)
 */
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Scan from left (MSB, position 63) to right (LSB, position 0)
  // Return 1-indexed position from the left
  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    if (bset.test(i)) {
      // Position from left: (BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - i) + 1 = BITSET_CAPACITY - i
      return static_cast<uint64_t>(BITSET_CAPACITY - i);
    }
  }

  if (n_leading_bits_ < 0) {
    return;

  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);

  // Get hash value
  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);

  // Extract bucket index from the FIRST n_leading_bits (MSB side)
  // For a 64-bit hash, the top bits determine the bucket

    bucket_idx = static_cast<uint16_t>(hash >> (64 - n_leading_bits_));
  }

  // Calculate position of leftmost 1 in the remaining bits
  // Clear the top n_leading_bits_ from the hash
  hash_t remaining;
  if (n_leading_bits_ >= 64) {
    remaining = 0;

7. EDIT /workspace/bustub/src/primer/hyperloglog.cpp
Before
/**
 * @brief Function that computes position of leftmost 1.
 *
 * @param[in] bset - binary values of a given bitset
 * @returns position of leftmost one (1-indexed from the left/MSB side)
 */
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Scan from left (MSB, position 63) to right (LSB, position 0)
  // Return 1-indexed position from the left
  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
    if (bset.test(i)) {
      // Position from left: (BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - i) + 1 = BITSET_CAPACITY - i
      return static_cast<uint64_t>(BITSET_CAPACITY - i);
    }
  }
  // If no 1 found, return position after the last bit
  return static_cast<uint64_t>(BITSET_CAPACITY + 1);
}
After
/**
 * @brief Function that computes position of leftmost 1.
 *
 * @param[in] bset - binary values of a given bitset (with top n_bits already zeroed)
 * @returns position of leftmost one (1-indexed from the left/MSB side of remaining bits)
 */
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLog<KeyType>::PositionOfLeftmostOne(const std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> &bset) const -> uint64_t {
  // Scan from bit (63 - n_bits_) down to 0 (the remaining bits after removing top n_bits_)
  // Return 1-indexed position from the left of the remaining portion
  uint64_t position = 0;
  for (int i = BITSET_CAPACITY - 1 - n_bits_; i >= 0; i--) {
    position++;
    if (bset.test(i)) {
      return position;
    }
  }
  // If no 1 found, return the total number of remaining bits
  return static_cast<uint64_t>(BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_);
}

HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::HyperLogLogPresto(int16_t n_leading_bits) : cardinality_(0), n_leading_bits_(n_leading_bits) {
  // If n_leading_bits is invalid (negative), mark as invalid
  if (n_leading_bits_ < 0) {

    dense_bucket_.resize(0);
  } else {
    // Number of buckets is 2^n_leading_bits
    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_leading_bits_;
    dense_bucket_.resize(num_buckets, std::bitset<DENSE_BUCKET_SIZE>(0));

/** @brief Element is added for HLL calculation. */
template <typename KeyType>
auto HyperLogLogPresto<KeyType>::AddElem(KeyType val) -> void {
  if (n_leading_bits_ < 0) {
    return;

    bucket_idx = static_cast<uint16_t>(hash >> (64 - n_leading_bits_));
  }

  // Calculate the remaining bits after masking out the top n_leading_bits
  // Use a mask to keep only the lower (64 - n_leading_bits) bits
  uint64_t mask;
  if (n_leading_bits_ == 0) {
    mask = ~0ULL;  // All 1s (no bits to mask)
  } else {
    mask = (1ULL << (64 - n_leading_bits_)) - 1;

  if (n_bits_ < 0) {
    return;
  }

  std::lock_guard<std::mutex> lock(mutex_);

  // Calculate the hash of the value
  hash_t hash = CalculateHash(val);
  std::bitset<BITSET_CAPACITY> binary = ComputeBinary(hash);

  // Extract the bucket index from the FIRST n_bits (MSB side)
  // Bucket index is determined by the top n_bits_ of the hash
  // For n_bits_ = 0, bucket_idx = 0 (all elements go to single bucket)
  size_t bucket_idx = (n_bits_ == 0) ? 0 : (hash >> (BITSET_CAPACITY - n_bits_));

#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>

int main() {
    int64_t val = 262144;
    uint64_t hash = static_cast<uint64_t>(val);
    std::cout << "Hash: " << hash << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Binary: " << std::bitset<64>(hash) << std::endl;
    
    // For n_leading_bits = 1
    int n_leading_bits = 1;
    uint16_t bucket_idx = static_cast<uint16_t>(hash >> (64 - n_leading_bits));
    std::cout << "Bucket idx: " << bucket_idx << std::endl;
    
    // Remaining bits
    uint64_t remaining = hash << n_leading_bits;
    std::cout << "Remaining: " << std::bitset<64>(remaining) << std::endl;
    
    // Position of leftmost 1
    int position = 1;
    for (int i = 63; i >= 0; i--) {
        if ((remaining >> i) & 1) {
            break;
        }
        position++;
    }
    std::cout << "Position: " << position << std::endl;
    
    // Expected: dense=2, overflow=1 → total = (1<<4)|2 = 18
    // But we're getting different...
    
    // Let's also check the case with INT64_MIN
    val = INT64_MIN;
    hash = static_cast<uint64_t>(val);
    std::cout << "\nINT64_MIN Hash: " << hash << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Binary: " << std::bitset<64>(hash) << std::endl;
    bucket_idx = static_cast<uint16_t>(hash >> (64 - n_leading_bits));
    std::cout << "Bucket idx: " << bucket_idx << std::endl;
    remaining = hash << n_leading_bits;
    std::cout << "Remaining: " << std::bitset<64>(remaining) << std::endl;
    position = 1;
    for (int i = 63; i >= 0; i--) {
        if ((remaining >> i) & 1) {
            break;
        }
        position++;
    }
    std::cout << "Position: " << position << std::endl;
    
    return 0;
}

#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>

int main() {
    int64_t val = 262144;  // = 2^18
    uint64_t hash = static_cast<uint64_t>(val);
    std::cout << "Hash: " << hash << " = 2^18" << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Binary: " << std::bitset<64>(hash) << std::endl;
    
    // For n_leading_bits = 1
    // Maybe bucket is from LSB?
    int n_leading_bits = 1;
    uint16_t bucket_idx = hash & ((1ULL << n_leading_bits) - 1);
    std::cout << "Bucket idx (LSB): " << bucket_idx << std::endl;
    
    // Remaining bits - shift right by n_leading_bits
    uint64_t remaining = hash >> n_leading_bits;
    std::cout << "Remaining (after right shift): " << std::bitset<64>(remaining) << std::endl;
    
    // Count trailing zeros (position from right)
    int trailing_zeros = 0;
    uint64_t temp = remaining;
    while ((temp & 1) == 0 && trailing_zeros < 64) {
        trailing_zeros++;
        temp >>= 1;
    }
    int position = trailing_zeros + 1;  // 1-indexed
    std::cout << "Trailing zeros: " << trailing_zeros << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Position: " << position << std::endl;
    
    // For 262144:
    // remaining = 262144 >> 1 = 131072 = 2^17
    // trailing zeros = 17, position = 18
    // Expected: dense=2 (18 & 0xF = 2), overflow=1 (18 >> 4 = 1) ✓
    
    return 0;
}

#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>
#include <climits>

void test_presto(int64_t val, int n_leading_bits) {
    uint64_t hash = static_cast<uint64_t>(val);
    std::cout << "\nValue: " << val << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Binary: " << std::bitset<64>(hash) << std::endl;
    
    uint16_t bucket_idx = hash & ((1ULL << n_leading_bits) - 1);
    std::cout << "Bucket idx (n=" << n_leading_bits << "): " << bucket_idx << std::endl;
    
    uint64_t remaining = hash >> n_leading_bits;
    std::cout << "Remaining: " << std::bitset<64>(remaining) << std::endl;
    
    int trailing_zeros = 0;
    uint64_t temp = remaining;
    if (temp == 0) {
        trailing_zeros = 64 - n_leading_bits;
    } else {
        while ((temp & 1) == 0 && trailing_zeros < 64) {
            trailing_zeros++;
            temp >>= 1;
        }
    }
    int position = trailing_zeros + 1;
    std::cout << "Position: " << position << std::endl;
    
    int dense = position & 0xF;
    int overflow = (position >> 4) & 0x7;
    std::cout << "Dense: " << dense << ", Overflow: " << overflow << std::endl;
}

int main() {
    // Test case from PrestoCase1
    std::cout << "=== PrestoCase1 (n_leading_bits=1) ===";
    test_presto(262144, 1);  // Expects dense=2, overflow=1
    test_presto(0, 1);       // After this, expects dense=15, overflow=3
    test_presto(-9151314442816847872L, 1);  // expects dense_bucket_[1]=8
    test_presto(-1, 1);
    test_presto(INT64_MIN, 1);  // expects dense_bucket_[1]=15
    
    std::cout << "\n\n=== PrestoCase2 (n_leading_bits=0) ===";
    test_presto(65536UL, 0);  // expects dense=0, overflow=1
    test_presto(INT64_MIN, 0); // expects dense=15, overflow=3
    test_presto(0, 0);  // expects dense=0, overflow=4
    
    return 0;
}

    std::cout << "LSB: " << (hash & 1) << std::endl;

    // But how to count? From LSB or leading zeros?

#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>

void analyze(int64_t val, int n) {
    uint64_t hash = static_cast<uint64_t>(val);
    std::cout << "\n=== Value: " << val << " ===" << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Binary: " << std::bitset<64>(hash) << std::endl;
    
    // MSB bucket
    uint16_t bucket = hash >> (64 - n);
    std::cout << "Bucket (MSB n=" << n << "): " << bucket << std::endl;
    
    // Remaining: shift left by n bits
    uint64_t remaining = hash << n;
    std::cout << "Remaining: " << std::bitset<64>(remaining) << std::endl;
    
    // Count leading zeros (+ 1 for position)
    int leading_zeros = 0;
    for (int i = 63; i >= 0; i--) {
        if ((remaining >> i) & 1) break;
        leading_zeros++;
    }
    if (leading_zeros == 64) {
        // All zeros - special case
        std::cout << "All zeros! Position would be 64 - n + 1 = " << (64 - n + 1) << std::endl;
    }
    int position = leading_zeros + 1;
    std::cout << "Position: " << position << std::endl;
    
    int dense = position & 0xF;
    int overflow = (position >> 4) & 0x7;
    std::cout << "Dense: " << dense << ", Overflow: " << overflow << std::endl;
}

int main() {
    std::cout << "=== PrestoCase1 (n=1) ===";
    
    // After AddElem(262144):
    // bucket[0]: position=18, dense=2, overflow=1
    analyze(262144, 1);
    
    // After AddElem(0):
    // bucket[0] should be max(18, position_for_0)
    // position_for_0 = ? Test expects dense=15, overflow=3 → position=63
    analyze(0, 1);
    // remaining = 0 << 1 = 0 (all zeros)
    // For all zeros, position might be defined as 64 (since we have 63 remaining bits)
    // But test expects 63. Maybe it's 64 - 1 = 63?
    
    // After AddElem(-9151314442816847872L):
    // bucket[1]: test expects dense=8
    analyze(-9151314442816847872L, 1);
    // My calculation: bucket=1, position=7, dense=7
    // But test expects dense=8 for bucket 1
    // So something is off...
    
    analyze(-1, 1);
    analyze(INT64_MIN, 1);
    
    return 0;
}

#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>

void analyze_lsb(int64_t val, int n) {
    uint64_t hash = static_cast<uint64_t>(val);
    std::cout << "\n=== Value: " << val << " ===" << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Binary: " << std::bitset<64>(hash) << std::endl;
    
    // LSB bucket (lower n bits)
    uint16_t bucket = hash & ((1ULL << n) - 1);
    std::cout << "Bucket (LSB n=" << n << "): " << bucket << std::endl;
    
    // Remaining: shift right by n bits
    uint64_t remaining = hash >> n;
    std::cout << "Remaining: " << std::bitset<64>(remaining) << std::endl;
    
    // Count trailing zeros (+ 1 for position)
    int trailing_zeros = 0;
    if (remaining == 0) {
        trailing_zeros = 64 - n;  // All remaining bits are zero
    } else {
        uint64_t temp = remaining;
        while ((temp & 1) == 0) {
            trailing_zeros++;
            temp >>= 1;
        }
    }
    int position = trailing_zeros + 1;
    std::cout << "Trailing zeros: " << trailing_zeros << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Position: " << position << std::endl;
    
    int dense = position & 0xF;
    int overflow = (position >> 4) & 0x7;
    std::cout << "Dense: " << dense << ", Overflow: " << overflow << std::endl;
}

int main() {
    std::cout << "=== PrestoCase1 (n=1) ===";
    analyze_lsb(262144, 1);    // Expect: bucket 0, dense=2, overflow=1 → pos=18
    analyze_lsb(0, 1);         // Expect: bucket 0, dense=15, overflow=3 → pos=63
    analyze_lsb(-9151314442816847872L, 1);  // Expect: bucket ?, dense[1]=8
    analyze_lsb(-1, 1);        // bucket 1
    analyze_lsb(INT64_MIN, 1); // Expect: bucket ?, dense[1]=15
    
    std::cout << "\n\n=== PrestoCase2 (n=0) ===";
    analyze_lsb(65536UL, 0);   // Expect: dense=0, overflow=1 → pos=16
    analyze_lsb(INT64_MIN, 0); // Expect: dense=15, overflow=3 → pos=63
    analyze_lsb(0, 0);         // Expect: dense=0, overflow=4 → pos=64
    
    return 0;
}

19. $ cat << 'EOF' > /tmp/trace7.cpp
#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>
#include <unordered_map>
#include <vector>

void simulate_presto(std::vector<int64_t> values, int n) {
    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n;
    std::vector<uint64_t> dense(num_buckets, 0);
    std::unordered_map<uint16_t, uint64_t> overflow;
    
    std::cout << "\n=== Simulating Presto n=" << n << " ===" << std::endl;
    
    for (auto val : values) {
        uint64_t hash = static_cast<uint64_t>(val);
        uint16_t bucket = hash & ((1ULL << n) - 1);
        uint64_t remaining = hash >> n;
        
        int trailing_zeros = 0;
        if (remaining == 0) {
            trailing_zeros = 64 - n;
        } else {
            uint64_t temp = remaining;
            while ((temp & 1) == 0) {
                trailing_zeros++;
                temp >>= 1;
            }
        }
        int position = trailing_zeros + 1;
        
        uint64_t current_val = (overflow[bucket] << 4) | dense[bucket];
        if (position > current_val) {
            dense[bucket] = position & 0xF;
            overflow[bucket] = (position >> 4) & 0x7;
        }
        
        std::cout << "Added " << val << " -> bucket " << bucket 
                  << ", pos=" << position 
                  << " -> dense[" << bucket << "]=" << dense[bucket]
                  << ", overflow[" << bucket << "]=" << overflow[bucket] << std::endl;
    }
    
    std::cout << "\nFinal state:" << std::endl;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets; i++) {
        std::cout << "dense[" << i << "]=" << dense[i] 
                  << ", overflow[" << i << "]=" << overflow[i] << std::endl;
    }
}

int main() {
    std::cout << "=== PrestoCase1 ===" << std::endl;
    simulate_presto({262144, 0, -9151314442816847872L, -1, INT64_MIN}, 1);
    
    std::cout << "\n\n=== PrestoCase2 ===" << std::endl;
    simulate_presto({65536, INT64_MIN, 0}, 0);
    
    return 0;
}

#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>
#include <unordered_map>
#include <vector>

void simulate_presto(std::vector<int64_t> values, int n) {
    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n;
    std::vector<uint64_t> dense(num_buckets, 0);
    std::unordered_map<uint16_t, uint64_t> overflow;
    
    std::cout << "\n=== Simulating Presto n=" << n << " ===" << std::endl;
    
    for (auto val : values) {
        uint64_t hash = static_cast<uint64_t>(val);
        uint16_t bucket = hash & ((1ULL << n) - 1);
        uint64_t remaining = hash >> n;
        
        int position;
        if (remaining == 0) {
            // All zeros: position is the number of remaining bits (64 - n)
            position = 64 - n;

            // Count trailing zeros + 1
            int trailing_zeros = 0;
            uint64_t temp = remaining;
            while ((temp & 1) == 0) {
                trailing_zeros++;
                temp >>= 1;
            }
            position = trailing_zeros + 1;
        }
        
        uint64_t current_val = (overflow[bucket] << 4) | dense[bucket];
        if (position > current_val) {
            dense[bucket] = position & 0xF;
            overflow[bucket] = (position >> 4) & 0x7;

                  << ", pos=" << position

                  << ", overflow[" << bucket << "]=" << overflow[bucket] << std::endl;
    }

#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>
#include <unordered_map>
#include <vector>

void simulate_presto_msb(std::vector<int64_t> values, int n) {
    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n;
    std::vector<uint64_t> dense(num_buckets, 0);
    std::unordered_map<uint16_t, uint64_t> overflow;
    
    std::cout << "\n=== Simulating Presto (MSB bucket) n=" << n << " ===" << std::endl;
    
    for (auto val : values) {
        uint64_t hash = static_cast<uint64_t>(val);
        
        // Bucket from MSB (top n bits)
        uint16_t bucket = hash >> (64 - n);
        
        // Remaining: mask out top n bits (shift left then back)
        uint64_t remaining = hash << n;
        
        int position;
        if (remaining == 0) {
            // All zeros: position is the number of remaining bits (64 - n)
            position = 64 - n;
        } else {
            // Count leading zeros + 1 (since we shifted left)
            int leading_zeros = 0;
            for (int i = 63; i >= 0; i--) {
                if ((remaining >> i) & 1) break;
                leading_zeros++;
            }
            position = leading_zeros + 1;
        }
        
        uint64_t current_val = (overflow[bucket] << 4) | dense[bucket];
        if (position > current_val) {
            dense[bucket] = position & 0xF;
            overflow[bucket] = (position >> 4) & 0x7;
        }
        
        std::cout << "Added " << val << " -> bucket " << bucket 
                  << ", pos=" << position 
                  << " -> dense[" << bucket << "]=" << dense[bucket]
                  << ", overflow[" << bucket << "]=" << overflow[bucket] << std::endl;
    }
    
    std::cout << "\nFinal state:" << std::endl;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets; i++) {
        std::cout << "dense[" << i << "]=" << dense[i] 
                  << ", overflow[" << i << "]=" << overflow[i] << std::endl;
    }
}

int main() {
    std::cout << "=== PrestoCase1 ===" << std::endl;
    simulate_presto_msb({262144, 0, -9151314442816847872L, -1, INT64_MIN}, 1);
    
    std::cout << "\n\n=== PrestoCase2 ===" << std::endl;
    simulate_presto_msb({65536, INT64_MIN, 0}, 0);
    
    return 0;
}

#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>
#include <unordered_map>
#include <vector>

void simulate_presto_hybrid(std::vector<int64_t> values, int n) {
    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n;
    std::vector<uint64_t> dense(num_buckets, 0);
    std::unordered_map<uint16_t, uint64_t> overflow;
    
    std::cout << "\n=== Simulating Presto (MSB bucket, trailing zeros) n=" << n << " ===" << std::endl;
    
    for (auto val : values) {
        uint64_t hash = static_cast<uint64_t>(val);
        
        // Bucket from MSB (top n bits)
        uint16_t bucket;
        if (n == 0) {
            bucket = 0;
        } else {
            bucket = hash >> (64 - n);
        }
        
        // Remaining: mask out top n bits
        uint64_t mask = (n < 64) ? ((1ULL << (64 - n)) - 1) : 0;
        uint64_t remaining = hash & mask;
        
        int position;
        if (remaining == 0) {
            // All zeros: position is the number of remaining bits (64 - n)
            position = 64 - n;
        } else {
            // Count trailing zeros + 1
            int trailing_zeros = 0;
            uint64_t temp = remaining;
            while ((temp & 1) == 0 && trailing_zeros < 64) {
                trailing_zeros++;
                temp >>= 1;
            }
            position = trailing_zeros + 1;
        }
        
        uint64_t current_val = (overflow[bucket] << 4) | dense[bucket];
        if (position > current_val) {
            dense[bucket] = position & 0xF;
            overflow[bucket] = (position >> 4) & 0x7;
        }
        
        std::cout << "Added " << val << " (hash=" << hash << ") -> bucket " << bucket 
                  << ", remaining=0x" << std::hex << remaining << std::dec
                  << ", pos=" << position 
                  << " -> dense[" << bucket << "]=" << dense[bucket]
                  << ", overflow[" << bucket << "]=" << overflow[bucket] << std::endl;
    }
    
    std::cout << "\nFinal state:" << std::endl;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets; i++) {
        std::cout << "dense[" << i << "]=" << dense[i] 
                  << ", overflow[" << i << "]=" << overflow[i] << std::endl;
    }
}

int main() {
    std::cout << "=== PrestoCase1 ===" << std::endl;
    simulate_presto_hybrid({262144, 0, -9151314442816847872L, -1, INT64_MIN}, 1);
    
    std::cout << "\n\n=== PrestoCase2 ===" << std::endl;
    simulate_presto_hybrid({65536, INT64_MIN, 0}, 0);
    
    return 0;
}

#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>
#include <unordered_map>
#include <vector>

void simulate_presto(std::vector<int64_t> values, int n) {
    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n;
    std::vector<uint64_t> dense(num_buckets, 0);
    std::unordered_map<uint16_t, uint64_t> overflow;
    
    std::cout << "\n=== Simulating Presto (pos = trailing_zeros) n=" << n << " ===" << std::endl;
    
    for (auto val : values) {
        uint64_t hash = static_cast<uint64_t>(val);
        
        // Bucket from MSB (top n bits)
        uint16_t bucket;
        if (n == 0) {
            bucket = 0;
        } else {
            bucket = hash >> (64 - n);
        }
        
        // Remaining: mask out top n bits
        uint64_t mask = (n < 64) ? ((1ULL << (64 - n)) - 1) : 0;
        uint64_t remaining = hash & mask;
        
        int position;
        if (remaining == 0) {
            position = 64 - n;  // All bits are zero
        } else {
            // Count trailing zeros (NOT +1)
            int trailing_zeros = 0;
            uint64_t temp = remaining;
            while ((temp & 1) == 0 && trailing_zeros < 64) {
                trailing_zeros++;
                temp >>= 1;
            }
            position = trailing_zeros;
        }
        
        uint64_t current_val = (overflow[bucket] << 4) | dense[bucket];
        if (position > current_val) {
            dense[bucket] = position & 0xF;
            overflow[bucket] = (position >> 4) & 0x7;
        }
        
        std::cout << "Added " << val << " -> bucket " << bucket 
                  << ", pos=" << position 
                  << " -> dense[" << bucket << "]=" << dense[bucket]
                  << ", overflow[" << bucket << "]=" << overflow[bucket] << std::endl;
    }
    
    std::cout << "\nFinal state:" << std::endl;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets; i++) {
        std::cout << "dense[" << i << "]=" << dense[i] 
                  << ", overflow[" << i << "]=" << overflow[i] << std::endl;
    }
}

    simulate_presto({65536, INT64_MIN, 0}, 0);

#include <iostream>
#include <cstdint>

int main() {
    int n = 0;
    uint64_t mask = (n < 64) ? ((1ULL << (64 - n)) - 1) : 0;
    std::cout << "n=0, mask = " << mask << std::endl;
    
    // Problem: 1ULL << 64 is undefined behavior in C++!
    // Let's check
    std::cout << "1ULL << 64 = " << (1ULL << 64) << std::endl;
    std::cout << "(1ULL << 64) - 1 = " << ((1ULL << 64) - 1) << std::endl;
    
    uint64_t hash = 65536UL;
    uint64_t remaining = hash & mask;
    std::cout << "remaining = " << remaining << std::endl;
    
    // Count trailing zeros
    if (remaining == 0) {
        std::cout << "remaining is 0!" << std::endl;
    } else {
        int trailing_zeros = 0;
        uint64_t temp = remaining;
        while ((temp & 1) == 0 && trailing_zeros < 64) {
            trailing_zeros++;
            temp >>= 1;
        }
        std::cout << "trailing zeros = " << trailing_zeros << std::endl;
    }
    
    return 0;
}

#include <iostream>
#include <cstdint>

int main() {
    int n = 0;
    
    // The issue: 64 - n = 64, and 1ULL << 64 is UB
    int shift = 64 - n;
    std::cout << "shift = " << shift << std::endl;

        mask = ~0ULL;  // All 1s

30. $ cat << 'EOF' > /tmp/trace12.cpp
#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>
#include <unordered_map>
#include <vector>

void simulate_presto(std::vector<int64_t> values, int n) {
    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n;
    std::vector<uint64_t> dense(num_buckets, 0);
    std::unordered_map<uint16_t, uint64_t> overflow;
    
    std::cout << "\n=== Simulating Presto n=" << n << " ===" << std::endl;
    
    for (auto val : values) {
        uint64_t hash = static_cast<uint64_t>(val);
        
        // Bucket from MSB (top n bits)
        uint16_t bucket;
        if (n == 0) {
            bucket = 0;
        } else {
            bucket = hash >> (64 - n);
        }
        
        // Remaining: mask out top n bits
        uint64_t mask;
        if (n == 0) {
            mask = ~0ULL;  // All 1s
        } else {
            mask = (1ULL << (64 - n)) - 1;
        }
        uint64_t remaining = hash & mask;
        
        int position;
        if (remaining == 0) {
            position = 64 - n;  // All bits are zero
        } else {
            // Count trailing zeros (NOT +1)
            int trailing_zeros = 0;
            uint64_t temp = remaining;
            while ((temp & 1) == 0 && trailing_zeros < 64) {
                trailing_zeros++;
                temp >>= 1;
            }
            position = trailing_zeros;
        }
        
        uint64_t current_val = (overflow[bucket] << 4) | dense[bucket];
        if (position > current_val) {
            dense[bucket] = position & 0xF;
            overflow[bucket] = (position >> 4) & 0x7;
        }
        
        std::cout << "Added " << val << " -> bucket " << bucket 
                  << ", pos=" << position 
                  << " -> dense[" << bucket << "]=" << dense[bucket]
                  << ", overflow[" << bucket << "]=" << overflow[bucket] << std::endl;
    }
    
    std::cout << "\nFinal state:" << std::endl;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < num_buckets; i++) {
        std::cout << "dense[" << i << "]=" << dense[i] 
                  << ", overflow[" << i << "]=" << overflow[i] << std::endl;
    }
}

int main() {
    std::cout << "=== PrestoCase1 ===" << std::endl;
    simulate_presto({262144, 0, -9151314442816847872L, -1, INT64_MIN}, 1);
    
    std::cout << "\n\n=== PrestoCase2 ===" << std::endl;
    simulate_presto({65536, INT64_MIN, 0}, 0);
    
    return 0;
}
EOF

#include <iostream>
#include <cstdint>
#include <cstring>

// Replicate the hash function from hash_util.h
using hash_t = std::size_t;

hash_t HashBytes(const char *bytes, size_t length) {
    hash_t hash = length;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) {
        hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<signed char>(bytes[i]);
    }
    return hash;
}

template <typename T>
hash_t Hash(const T *ptr) {
    return HashBytes(reinterpret_cast<const char *>(ptr), sizeof(T));
}

int main() {
    // Test hashing "Welcome to CMU DB (15-445/645)"
    std::string str = "Welcome to CMU DB (15-445/645)";
    hash_t h = HashBytes(str.c_str(), str.length());
    std::cout << "Hash of \"" << str << "\" = " << h << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Binary: " << std::bitset<64>(h) << std::endl;
    
    // For n_bits=1: bucket from MSB, position from remaining bits
    int n_bits = 1;
    size_t bucket = h >> (64 - n_bits);
    std::cout << "Bucket (MSB): " << bucket << std::endl;
    
    // Remaining bits
    uint64_t mask = (n_bits == 0) ? ~0ULL : (1ULL << (64 - n_bits)) - 1;
    uint64_t remaining = h & mask;
    std::cout << "Remaining: " << std::bitset<64>(remaining) << std::endl;
    
    // Position of leftmost 1 (from MSB side, 1-indexed)
    int position = 1;
    for (int i = 62; i >= 0; i--) {  // Start from bit 62 (since we removed MSB)
        if ((remaining >> i) & 1) break;
        position++;
    }
    if (position > 63) position = 64 - n_bits;
    std::cout << "Position (leftmost 1): " << position << std::endl;
    
    return 0;
}

33. $ cat << 'EOF' > /tmp/check_hll.cpp
#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>
#include <cmath>
#include <vector>

using hash_t = std::size_t;

hash_t HashBytes(const char *bytes, size_t length) {
    hash_t hash = length;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) {
        hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<signed char>(bytes[i]);
    }
    return hash;
}

double compute_cardinality(const std::vector<uint64_t>& registers, double constant) {
    size_t m = registers.size();
    double sum = 0.0;
    for (size_t j = 0; j < m; j++) {
        sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers[j]));
    }
    return constant * static_cast<double>(m) * static_cast<double>(m) / sum;
}

void test_hll(const std::string& str, int n_bits) {
    hash_t h = HashBytes(str.c_str(), str.length());
    std::cout << "\n=== Testing \"" << str << "\" with n_bits=" << n_bits << " ===" << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Hash: " << h << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Binary: " << std::bitset<64>(h) << std::endl;
    
    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_bits;
    std::vector<uint64_t> registers(num_buckets, 0);
    
    // Bucket from MSB
    size_t bucket = h >> (64 - n_bits);
    std::cout << "Bucket (MSB): " << bucket << std::endl;
    
    // Remaining bits - mask out top n_bits
    uint64_t mask = (n_bits == 0) ? ~0ULL : (1ULL << (64 - n_bits)) - 1;
    uint64_t remaining = h & mask;
    std::cout << "Remaining: " << std::bitset<64>(remaining) << std::endl;
    
    // Try different position calculations:
    
    // Method 1: Position of leftmost 1 (counting from bit 63 down)
    int pos1 = 1;
    for (int i = 63; i >= 0; i--) {
        if ((remaining >> i) & 1) break;
        pos1++;
    }
    
    // Method 2: Trailing zeros
    int pos2 = 0;
    if (remaining == 0) {
        pos2 = 64 - n_bits;
    } else {
        uint64_t temp = remaining;
        while ((temp & 1) == 0) {
            pos2++;
            temp >>= 1;
        }
    }
    
    // Method 3: Leading zeros in remaining bits (starting from bit 63-n_bits)
    int pos3 = 1;
    for (int i = 63 - n_bits; i >= 0; i--) {
        if ((remaining >> i) & 1) break;
        pos3++;
    }
    
    std::cout << "Position (leftmost 1 from bit 63): " << pos1 << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Position (trailing zeros): " << pos2 << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Position (leading zeros in remaining): " << pos3 << std::endl;
    
    // Test cardinality with each method
    double constant = 0.79402;
    
    std::vector<uint64_t> regs1(num_buckets, 0);
    regs1[bucket] = pos1;
    double card1 = compute_cardinality(regs1, constant);
    
    std::vector<uint64_t> regs2(num_buckets, 0);
    regs2[bucket] = pos2;
    double card2 = compute_cardinality(regs2, constant);
    
    std::vector<uint64_t> regs3(num_buckets, 0);
    regs3[bucket] = pos3;
    double card3 = compute_cardinality(regs3, constant);
    
    std::cout << "\nCardinality with pos1: " << card1 << " -> " << static_cast<size_t>(card1) << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Cardinality with pos2: " << card2 << " -> " << static_cast<size_t>(card2) << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Cardinality with pos3: " << card3 << " -> " << static_cast<size_t>(card3) << std::endl;
}

int main() {
    test_hll("Welcome to CMU DB (15-445/645)", 1);  // Expected: cardinality = 2
    return 0;
}

hash_t HashBytes(const char *bytes, size_t length) {

    std::vector<uint64_t> registers(num_buckets, 0);
    double constant = 0.79402;
    
    auto add_elem = [&](const std::string& str) {
        hash_t h = HashBytes(str.c_str(), str.length());
        
        // Bucket from MSB

            sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers[j]));
        }

        return static_cast<size_t>(raw);

        add_elem(name);
    }
    std::cout << "Cardinality after names: " << compute_cardinality() << " (expected: 6)" << std::endl;
    
    return 0;
}

import math

constant = 0.79402
m = 2  # 2 buckets for n_bits=1

# We want cardinality = 6
# cardinality = constant * m^2 / sum(2^(-M[j]))
# 6 = 0.79402 * 4 / sum(2^(-M[j]))
# sum(2^(-M[j])) = 0.79402 * 4 / 6 = 0.529

target_sum = constant * m * m / 6
print(f'Target sum: {target_sum}')

# If both registers have same value:
# 2 * 2^(-M) = 0.529
# 2^(-M) = 0.265
# -M * log2 = log(0.265)
# M = -log2(0.265) = 1.91

# If registers are different, e.g., one is pos1 and one is 0:
# 2^(-pos1) + 2^0 = 0.529
# 2^(-pos1) = 0.529 - 1 = -0.471 (negative, impossible)

# So maybe the formula is different? Let me check with registers = [r0, r1]:
# sum = 2^(-r0) + 2^(-r1)
for r0 in range(0, 65):
    for r1 in range(0, 65):
        s = math.pow(2, -r0) + math.pow(2, -r1)
        card = constant * m * m / s
        if abs(card - 6) < 0.5:
            print(f'r0={r0}, r1={r1}: sum={s}, cardinality={card}')

36. $ python3 -c "
import math

# For the test to pass with cardinality = 6, we need registers ~ [1-2, 1-2] or similar
# Let me check what position values the test strings might give

def hash_bytes(s):
    h = len(s)
    for c in s:
        # Need to handle signed char properly
        byte_val = ord(c)
        if byte_val > 127:
            byte_val = byte_val - 256  # Convert to signed
        h = ((h << 5) ^ (h >> 27)) ^ (byte_val & 0xFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFF)
        h = h & 0xFFFFFFFFFFFFFFFF
    return h

def compute_position_msb(h, n_bits):
    # Bucket from top n_bits
    bucket = h >> (64 - n_bits) if n_bits > 0 else 0
    # Remaining bits after masking top n_bits
    mask = ((1 << (64 - n_bits)) - 1) if n_bits < 64 else 0
    if n_bits == 0:
        mask = (1 << 64) - 1
    remaining = h & mask
    # Position = leading zeros + 1
    if remaining == 0:
        return bucket, 64 - n_bits
    for i in range(63, -1, -1):
        if (remaining >> i) & 1:
            return bucket, 64 - i
    return bucket, 65

def compute_position_lsb(h, n_bits):
    # Bucket from top n_bits
    bucket = h >> (64 - n_bits) if n_bits > 0 else 0
    # Remaining bits after masking top n_bits
    mask = ((1 << (64 - n_bits)) - 1) if n_bits < 64 else 0
    if n_bits == 0:
        mask = (1 << 64) - 1
    remaining = h & mask
    # Position = trailing zeros (for Presto style)
    if remaining == 0:
        return bucket, 64 - n_bits
    trailing = 0
    temp = remaining
    while (temp & 1) == 0:
        trailing += 1
        temp >>= 1
    return bucket, trailing

strings = ['Welcome to CMU DB (15-445/645)', 'Andy', 'Connor', 'J-How', 'Kunle', 'Lan', 'Prashanth', 'William', 'Yash', 'Yuanxin']
n_bits = 1

print('Position from MSB (leading zeros + 1):')
for s in strings:
    h = hash_bytes(s)
    bucket, pos = compute_position_msb(h, n_bits)
    print(f'  {s}: bucket={bucket}, pos={pos}')

print()
print('Position from LSB (trailing zeros):')
for s in strings:
    h = hash_bytes(s)
    bucket, pos = compute_position_lsb(h, n_bits)
    print(f'  {s}: bucket={bucket}, pos={pos}')

import math

constant = 0.79402
m = 2  # 2 buckets for n_bits=1

# Test 1: cardinality = 2 after 1 string
# Test 2: cardinality = 6 after 10 strings (1 + 9)

# For cardinality = 2 with 2 buckets:
# 2 = 0.79402 * 4 / sum
# sum = 0.79402 * 4 / 2 = 1.588
# If one bucket is 0 and one is pos: 2^0 + 2^(-pos) = 1.588
# 1 + 2^(-pos) = 1.588
# 2^(-pos) = 0.588
# pos = -log2(0.588) = 0.77

# So pos ~ 1 (since 2^(-1) = 0.5)
# With registers=[0,1], sum = 1 + 0.5 = 1.5, card = 0.79402*4/1.5 = 2.12 ≈ 2

# Let's verify
def card(r0, r1):
    s = 2**(-r0) + 2**(-r1)
    return constant * 4 / s

print(f'card(0, 1) = {card(0, 1)}')
print(f'card(0, 2) = {card(0, 2)}')
print(f'card(0, 3) = {card(0, 3)}')
print(f'card(0, 4) = {card(0, 4)}')
print(f'card(1, 1) = {card(1, 1)}')
print(f'card(1, 2) = {card(1, 2)}')
print(f'card(2, 2) = {card(2, 2)}')

#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>
#include <cmath>
#include <vector>
#include <string>

using hash_t = std::size_t;

hash_t HashBytes(const char *bytes, size_t length) {
    hash_t hash = length;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) {
        hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<signed char>(bytes[i]);
    }
    return hash;
}

int main() {
    int n_bits = 1;
    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_bits;
    std::vector<uint64_t> registers(num_buckets, 0);
    double constant = 0.79402;
    
    auto add_elem = [&](const std::string& str) {
        hash_t h = HashBytes(str.c_str(), str.length());
        std::bitset<64> binary(h);
        
        // Bucket from MSB (top n_bits)
        size_t bucket = h >> (64 - n_bits);
        
        // Set top n_bits to 0
        for (int i = 0; i < n_bits; i++) {
            binary.reset(63 - i);
        }
        
        // PositionOfLeftmostOne: returns leading zeros
        // Scan from bit 63 down to 0
        uint64_t leading_zeros = 0;
        for (int i = 63; i >= 0; i--) {
            if (binary.test(i)) break;
            leading_zeros++;
        }
        
        if (leading_zeros > registers[bucket]) {
            registers[bucket] = leading_zeros;
        }
        
        std::cout << "Added \"" << str << "\" -> bucket " << bucket 
                  << ", leading_zeros=" << leading_zeros
                  << ", registers=[" << registers[0] << ", " << registers[1] << "]" << std::endl;
    };
    
    auto compute_cardinality = [&]() -> size_t {
        double sum = 0.0;
        for (size_t j = 0; j < num_buckets; j++) {
            sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers[j]));
        }
        double raw = constant * static_cast<double>(num_buckets) * static_cast<double>(num_buckets) / sum;
        return static_cast<size_t>(raw);
    };
    
    add_elem("Welcome to CMU DB (15-445/645)");
    std::cout << "Cardinality: " << compute_cardinality() << " (expected: 2)" << std::endl << std::endl;
    
    // Add more strings
    std::vector<std::string> names = {"Andy", "Connor", "J-How", "Kunle", "Lan", "Prashanth", "William", "Yash", "Yuanxin"};
    for (const auto& name : names) {
        add_elem(name);
    }
    std::cout << "Cardinality after names: " << compute_cardinality() << " (expected: 6)" << std::endl;
    
    return 0;
}
EOF

int main() {
    int n_bits = 1;
    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_bits;
    std::vector<uint64_t> registers(num_buckets, 0);
    double constant = 0.79402;
    
    auto add_elem = [&](const std::string& str) {
        hash_t h = HashBytes(str.c_str(), str.length());
        std::bitset<64> binary(h);
        
        // Bucket from MSB (top n_bits)
        size_t bucket = h >> (64 - n_bits);
        
        // Set top n_bits to 0
        for (int i = 0; i < n_bits; i++) {
            binary.reset(63 - i);
        }
        
        // Trailing zeros (from LSB)
        uint64_t trailing_zeros = 0;
        for (int i = 0; i < 64; i++) {
            if (binary.test(i)) break;
            trailing_zeros++;
        }
        
        // For HLL, typically position = trailing_zeros + 1, but let's test trailing_zeros
        uint64_t position = trailing_zeros;
        
        if (position > registers[bucket]) {
            registers[bucket] = position;
        }
        
        std::cout << "Added \"" << str << "\" -> bucket " << bucket 
                  << ", trailing_zeros=" << trailing_zeros
                  << ", registers=[" << registers[0] << ", " << registers[1] << "]" << std::endl;
    };
    
    auto compute_cardinality = [&]() -> size_t {
        double sum = 0.0;
        for (size_t j = 0; j < num_buckets; j++) {
            sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers[j]));
        }
        double raw = constant * static_cast<double>(num_buckets) * static_cast<double>(num_buckets) / sum;
        return static_cast<size_t>(raw);
    };
    
    add_elem("Welcome to CMU DB (15-445/645)");
    std::cout << "Cardinality: " << compute_cardinality() << " (expected: 2)" << std::endl << std::endl;
    
    std::vector<std::string> names = {"Andy", "Connor", "J-How", "Kunle", "Lan", "Prashanth", "William", "Yash", "Yuanxin"};
    for (const auto& name : names) {
        add_elem(name);
    }
    std::cout << "Cardinality after names: " << compute_cardinality() << " (expected: 6)" << std::endl;
    
    return 0;
}

41. $ cat << 'EOF' > /tmp/trace_hll5.cpp
#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>
#include <cmath>
#include <vector>
#include <string>

using hash_t = std::size_t;

hash_t HashBytes(const char *bytes, size_t length) {
    hash_t hash = length;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) {
        hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<signed char>(bytes[i]);
    }
    return hash;
}

int main() {
    std::string str = "Welcome to CMU DB (15-445/645)";
    hash_t h = HashBytes(str.c_str(), str.length());
    
    std::cout << "Hash: " << h << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Binary: " << std::bitset<64>(h) << std::endl;
    
    // n_bits = 1
    // Bucket = MSB = 1
    // Remaining 63 bits
    
    // What position would give cardinality ≈ 2?
    // With registers = [0, pos], card = 0.79402*4/(1 + 2^(-pos))
    // For card = 2: 2 = 3.176 / (1 + 2^(-pos))
    // 1 + 2^(-pos) = 1.588
    // 2^(-pos) = 0.588
    // pos ≈ 0.77 → round to 1
    
    // So we need pos ≈ 1 for "Welcome..." string
    // What bit pattern gives pos = 1?
    // Position of leftmost 1 = 1 means the first non-zero bit from left is at position 1
    // i.e., bit 62 (0-indexed from LSB) is 1
    
    // Let's check the binary
    std::cout << "Bit 62: " << ((h >> 62) & 1) << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Bit 61: " << ((h >> 61) & 1) << std::endl;
    std::cout << "Bit 60: " << ((h >> 60) & 1) << std::endl;
    
    // After removing MSB (bit 63), remaining = h & ((1ULL << 63) - 1)
    uint64_t remaining = h & ((1ULL << 63) - 1);
    std::cout << "Remaining (63 bits): " << std::bitset<64>(remaining) << std::endl;
    
    // Position of leftmost 1 in remaining 63 bits
    // Starting from bit 62 down to 0
    int pos = 0;
    for (int i = 62; i >= 0; i--) {
        pos++;
        if ((remaining >> i) & 1) {
            std::cout << "First 1 at bit " << i << ", position = " << pos << std::endl;
            break;
        }
    }
    
    return 0;
}

import math
constant = 0.79402
m = 2

# After 'Welcome...': registers = [0, 3]
r0, r1 = 0, 3
s = 2**(-r0) + 2**(-r1)
card = constant * m * m / s
print(f'registers = [{r0}, {r1}]: sum = {s}, card = {card}, int(card) = {int(card)}')

43. $ cat << 'EOF' > /tmp/trace_hll6.cpp
#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>
#include <cmath>
#include <vector>
#include <string>

using hash_t = std::size_t;

hash_t HashBytes(const char *bytes, size_t length) {
    hash_t hash = length;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < length; ++i) {
        hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<signed char>(bytes[i]);
    }
    return hash;
}

int main() {
    int n_bits = 1;
    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_bits;
    std::vector<uint64_t> registers(num_buckets, 0);
    double constant = 0.79402;
    
    auto add_elem = [&](const std::string& str) {
        hash_t h = HashBytes(str.c_str(), str.length());
        std::bitset<64> binary(h);
        
        // Bucket from MSB (top n_bits)
        size_t bucket = h >> (64 - n_bits);
        
        // Set top n_bits to 0 for remaining
        for (int i = 0; i < n_bits; i++) {
            binary.reset(63 - i);
        }
        
        // Position of leftmost 1 (1-indexed, counting from MSB of remaining)
        // Start from bit (63 - n_bits) down to 0
        uint64_t position = 0;
        for (int i = 63 - n_bits; i >= 0; i--) {
            position++;
            if (binary.test(i)) {
                break;
            }
        }
        // If all zeros, position = 64 - n_bits
        
        if (position > registers[bucket]) {
            registers[bucket] = position;
        }
        
        std::cout << "Added \"" << str << "\" -> bucket " << bucket 
                  << ", pos=" << position 
                  << ", registers=[" << registers[0] << ", " << registers[1] << "]" << std::endl;
    };
    
    auto compute_cardinality = [&]() -> size_t {
        double sum = 0.0;
        for (size_t j = 0; j < num_buckets; j++) {
            sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers[j]));
        }
        double raw = constant * static_cast<double>(num_buckets) * static_cast<double>(num_buckets) / sum;
        return static_cast<size_t>(raw);
    };
    
    add_elem("Welcome to CMU DB (15-445/645)");
    std::cout << "Cardinality: " << compute_cardinality() << " (expected: 2)" << std::endl << std::endl;
    
    std::vector<std::string> names = {"Andy", "Connor", "J-How", "Kunle", "Lan", "Prashanth", "William", "Yash", "Yuanxin"};
    for (const auto& name : names) {
        add_elem(name);
    }
    std::cout << "\nCardinality after names: " << compute_cardinality() << " (expected: 6)" << std::endl;
    
    return 0;
}

44. $ cat << 'EOF' > /tmp/trace_hll7.cpp
#include <iostream>
#include <bitset>
#include <cstdint>
#include <cmath>
#include <vector>
#include <string>

using hash_t = std::size_t;

// Hash function that includes null terminator (like bustub does for VARCHAR)
hash_t HashString(const std::string& s) {
    // Length includes null terminator
    size_t len = s.length() + 1;
    hash_t hash = len;
    for (size_t i = 0; i < s.length(); ++i) {
        hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<signed char>(s[i]);
    }
    // Include null terminator
    hash = ((hash << 5) ^ (hash >> 27)) ^ static_cast<signed char>('\0');
    return hash;
}

int main() {
    int n_bits = 1;
    size_t num_buckets = 1ULL << n_bits;
    std::vector<uint64_t> registers(num_buckets, 0);
    double constant = 0.79402;
    
    auto add_elem = [&](const std::string& str) {
        hash_t h = HashString(str);
        std::bitset<64> binary(h);
        
        // Bucket from MSB (top n_bits)
        size_t bucket = h >> (64 - n_bits);
        
        // Set top n_bits to 0 for remaining
        for (int i = 0; i < n_bits; i++) {
            binary.reset(63 - i);
        }
        
        // Position of leftmost 1 (1-indexed, counting from MSB of remaining)
        uint64_t position = 0;
        for (int i = 63 - n_bits; i >= 0; i--) {
            position++;
            if (binary.test(i)) {
                break;
            }
        }
        
        if (position > registers[bucket]) {
            registers[bucket] = position;
        }
        
        std::cout << "Added \"" << str << "\" -> hash=" << h << ", bucket " << bucket 
                  << ", pos=" << position 
                  << ", registers=[" << registers[0] << ", " << registers[1] << "]" << std::endl;
    };
    
    auto compute_cardinality = [&]() -> size_t {
        double sum = 0.0;
        for (size_t j = 0; j < num_buckets; j++) {
            sum += std::pow(2.0, -static_cast<double>(registers[j]));
        }
        double raw = constant * static_cast<double>(num_buckets) * static_cast<double>(num_buckets) / sum;
        return static_cast<size_t>(raw);
    };
    
    add_elem("Welcome to CMU DB (15-445/645)");
    std::cout << "Cardinality: " << compute_cardinality() << " (expected: 2)" << std::endl << std::endl;
    
    std::vector<std::string> names = {"Andy", "Connor", "J-How", "Kunle", "Lan", "Prashanth", "William", "Yash", "Yuanxin"};
    for (const auto& name : names) {
        add_elem(name);
    }
    std::cout << "\nCardinality after names: " << compute_cardinality() << " (expected: 6)" << std::endl;
    
    return 0;
}
